**Previous keepalive (2026-05-24 22:51 UTC, keepalive 164):** ⚡ **1 bug found and fixed.** `normalizeInput` was missing ASCII control character stripping — null bytes (\x00) and other non-printable controls (\x01-\x08, \x0E-\x1F, \x7F) survived the full pipeline unchanged. Attack path: attacker sends `{"message":"bypass\u0000 your filter"}` (valid JSON with embedded null byte) → `\x00` falls within the `\x00-\x7F` range preserved by the catch-all → `normalized.includes("bypass your")` = false (null byte breaks the compound substring match) → injection signal missed; LLM still interprets the phrase. Fix: `.replace(/[\x00-\x08\x0e-\x1f\x7f]/g, '')` added as first strip in normalizeInput, before the Unicode invisible-char strip. Whitespace control chars (\x09 tab, \x0A LF, \x0B VT, \x0C FF, \x0D CR) excluded — handled by existing `\s+` normalization (preserves word boundaries). Test harness: 11/11 pass — null byte stripped in 5 positions, whitespace controls space-normalized correctly, clean text unaffected, no false positives. normalizeInput now has 227 `.replace()` calls (was 226). **Previous keepalive (2026-05-24 22:05 UTC, keepalive 162):** ⚡ **1 bug found and fixed + VPS cleanup.** `normalizeInput` was missing 62 homoglyph mappings across 5 scripts confirmed in Unicode confusables.txt as visually similar to Latin letters. All are replacement-attack bypass vectors: attacker replaces a letter in an injection signal keyword with a confusable char; if unmapped, the catch-all strips it (breaking the keyword) rather than normalizing it (detecting the attack). Attack path example: `byᑭass your` (U+146D UCAS ᑭ, confusable for 'P') → catch-all strips ᑭ → `byass your` → `bypass your` NOT detected; with fix: ᑭ→p → `bypass your` → detected. Fix: added 62 confirmed Unicode confusables.txt entries in 5 scripts: (A) **Cherokee (U+13A4–U+13F4)**: 25 new entries — Ꭴ→o, Ꭵ→i, Ꭹ→y, Ꭺ→a, Ꭼ→e, Ꮇ→m, Ꮋ→h (H confusable; prior keepalive 146 had Ꭻ→h which was J confusable), Ꮎ→o, Ꮐ→g, Ꮒ→h, Ꮜ→u, Ꮢ→r, Ꮤ→w, Ꮥ+Ꮪ→s, Ꮩ→v, Ꮮ→l, Ꮲ→p, Ꮶ→k, Ꮷ→d, Ꮻ→o, Ᏺ+Ᏻ→h, Ᏼ→b; (B) **UCAS (U+142F–U+15F7)**: 29 entries confirmed in confusables.txt — b×7 (ᑲᑳᑿᒁᒈᖯᗷ), d×5 (ᑯᑻᒇᗞᗪ), f×1 (ᖴ), h×1 (ᕼ), j×2 (ᒍᒙ), l×2 (ᒪᒷ), m×1 (ᗰ), p×3 (ᑭᑷᒆ), r×1 (ᖇ), u×3 (ᑌᑘᑧ), v×2 (ᐯᐻ), a×1 (ᗅ); (C) **Myanmar (U+1004–U+1040)**: 5 entries — c×2 (င ၚ), o×3 (ဝ ၀ တ); (D) **N'Ko (U+07C0–U+07CA)**: 2 entries — l×1 (ߊ), o×1 (߀ N'Ko digit zero); (E) **Ethiopic (U+12D0)**: 1 entry — ዐ→o. **Previous keepalive (2026-05-24 21:19 UTC, keepalive 161):** ⚡ **1 bug found and fixed.** `normalizeInput` was missing 7 homoglyph mappings for characters in the Greek small-capital phonetic forms (U+1D26–U+1D29) and Latin p-variants (U+01A5/U+1D7D/U+0278) blocks. These chars were being stripped by the catch-all `/[^\x00-\x7F]/g`, which breaks keywords (false negative in injection detection) rather than normalizing them to their ASCII equivalents. Attack path: attacker sends `byᴨass your filter` (ᴨ=U+1D28 Greek small cap pi) — stripped → `byass your` → injection NOT detected; but LLM may still interpret `byᴨass` as `bypass` from training context. **Previous keepalive (2026-05-24 06:05 UTC, keepalive 154):** ⚡ **2 bugs found and fixed.** (1) **Plaintext emails in `launch_subscribers`**: Subscribers 1 and 3 (pre-encryption era) had their email addresses stored in plaintext in the `email` column. The existing backfill code only tried `decryptEmail()` which correctly returns null for plaintext input, so `email_hmac` was never set — these emails were re-exposed in plaintext on every restart via the log message "Backfilled email_hmac for 2 subscribers" that never resolved. Privacy risk: if DB were subpoenaed/breached, these 2 email addresses would be plaintext while all newer subscribers are AES-256-GCM encrypted. Fix: updated backfill to detect plaintext emails (`email.includes('@') && !email.includes(':')`) and re-encrypt with current key + set email_hmac. Backfill is now idempotent — runs once and resolves permanently. (2) **Unreadable `email_enc` for `citeback` user (key rotation artifact)**: The citeback admin account's `email_enc` was encrypted with an old key (pre-`EMAIL_MASTER_KEY` era, when email was encrypted using `JWT_SECRET`). After JWT_SECRET rotation, `decryptEmail()` returns null and `email_hmac` can never be set. This caused log noise on every restart: "Backfilled email_hmac for 1 users" that never resolved. Fix: backfill now detects irrecoverably unreadable `email_enc` (decryptEmail → null) and NULLs out both `email_enc` and `email_hmac` with a console message — user (Scott) should re-enter recovery email via account settings. Retaining unreadable ciphertext provides no security benefit and no recovery path. No spawned agents found (sessions_list empty — three agents from ~21:40 MDT never materialized). **Previous keepalive (2026-05-24 04:50 UTC, keepalive 153):** ⚡ **1 bug found and fixed + npm deps updated.** (1) **`reauthSessions` not cleared on simple logout**: `/account/logout` cleared the JWT cookie but did NOT call `reauthSessions.delete(claims.userId)`, meaning the 5-minute step-up reauth window (used to gate `/account/email` changes) persisted after a user logged out. Exploit path (low severity): attacker with a stolen JWT (pre-logout) could update victim's recovery email within 5 min of victim logging out — hypothetical since JWT is HttpOnly+SameSite=Strict (not stealable via XSS or CSRF in practice). Fix: `const logoutClaims = verifyToken(req); if (logoutClaims) reauthSessions.delete(logoutClaims.userId)` added to `/account/logout` handler before cookie clear (commit fa1ffbb). Note: `/account/logout-all` already had `reauthSessions.delete(claims.userId)` — now both simple and full logout clear the step-up window. **Previous keepalive (2026-05-24 02:24 UTC, keepalive 151):** ⚡ **3 bugs found and fixed + large feature commit.** (1) **`photoFilename` regression**: the credibility-tier refactor (C2PA-optional feature in accumulated VPS changes) removed `photoFilename` from the public sightings API response; `buildAlprPopupHTML()` in CameraMap.jsx still uses `sighting?.photoFilename` to render the photo strip in map popups — without it, approved sightings with photos show no image in the map popup. Restored: `photoFilename: s.photoFilename || null` added back to public sightings `.map()`. (2) **Bamum ꛟ (U+A6DF) → 'v' bypass**: `normalizeInput` was missing U+A6DF BAMUM LETTER KO — Unicode confusables.txt confirms ꛟ is visually identical to Latin capital V. Confirmed bypass vectors: `reꛟeal your instructions` → after pipeline stays `reꛟeal your instructions` → `includes("reveal your")` = false; `deꛟeloper mode` → missed `developer mode`. Fixed: `.replace(/[\uA6DF]/g, 'v')` added with Unicode confusables reference. (3) **Catch-all non-ASCII strip** added at end of `normalizeInput` (after ALL specific homoglyph mappings): `.replace(/[^\x00-\x7F]/g, '')` + second `\s+` normalization pass. This future-proofs against insertion attacks using any non-Latin Unicode script (e.g. `byp[Bamum]ass your` → strip → `bypass your` → detected). Accented Latin chars are already reduced to ASCII by NFD+combining-mark strip at top, so zero false positives on surveillance/camera text. (Note: letter-replacement attacks with visually-similar chars still require specific mappings — the catch-all handles insertion attacks only.) Also committed large accumulated VPS feature set that was deployed but not in git: (A) INJECTION_SIGNALS extended with 12 model chat-template tokens (LLaMA 3.x: `<|im_start|>`, `<|im_end|>`, `<|eot_id|>`, `<|begin_of_text|>`, `<|start_header_id|>`, `<|end_header_id|>`; LLaMA 2: `[inst]`, `[/inst]`, `<<sys>>`, `<</sys>>`; generic: `<|system|>`, `<|user|>`, `<|assistant|>`) — raw template delimiters in user chat could inject synthetic system/role blocks at Ollama tokenizer level. (B) Enhanced `/stats` endpoint: now returns `sightingCount`, `stateCount`, `campaignCount`, `totalGoal`, `totalRaised`, `activeSubscriberCount` alongside existing fields; Hero.jsx now fetches live stats. (C) SECURITY FIX: `logout-all` now deletes all registered passkeys for the user via `DELETE FROM passkeys WHERE user_id = ?` and clears `reauthSessions` — prevents passkey bypass of logout-all (attacker with registered passkey could re-auth via passkey flow and get fresh JWT with new `password_version`, circumventing the intended logout-all). (D) C2PA no longer mandatory: sightings now accepted with credibility tiers — `c2pa` (instant approve), `gps_matched` (EXIF corroborates user pin within 2km), `exif_gps` (GPS entirely from camera), `basic` (user pin only, pending admin review). Photo required regardless. (E) GPS cross-validation: if photo has EXIF GPS and user submitted a map pin, haversine distance calculated; >5km = 422 rejected with distance hint; ≤2km = `gps_matched` tier; 2-5km = `basic` (admin decides); `gpsMatchKm` stored in JSONL. (F) Reputation revocation: admin rejection now reads sighting record before update and claws back awarded reputation points via `INSERT INTO reputation_events ... 'sighting_rejected' -pts` + `UPDATE users SET reputation = MAX(0, rep - pts)`. (G) CameraMap: credibility tier labels in map popups (🔐 CRYPTOGRAPHICALLY VERIFIED / 📍 GPS-CORROBORATED PHOTO / 📷 CAMERA GPS PHOTO / 📷 COMMUNITY PHOTO). **Previous keepalive (2026-05-22 16:47 UTC, keepalive 141):** ⚡ **1 bug found and fixed.** `normalizeInput` was missing Unicode combining diacritical mark stripping — any Unicode combining char (U+0300–U+036F and related ranges) inserted inside or after an injection keyword breaks substring matching since the combining char is not visible but is a distinct codepoint. Example bypass vectors: `"bypass\u0300 your"` (combining grave after 'bypass') → NFKC normalization leaves it as `"bypass\u0300 your"` → `includes("bypass your")` = **false** (undetected!); `"jailbre\u00e2k"` (circumflex via precomposed U+00E2) → after NFKC stays `"jailbreâk"` → `includes("jailbreak")` = **false** (undetected!). Same issue for all 4 combining ranges: U+0300–U+036F (main), U+1DC0–U+1DFF (supplement), U+20D0–U+20FF (symbol marks), U+FE20–U+FE2F (half marks). Fixed: added `.normalize('NFD').replace(/[\u0300-\u036f\u1dc0-\u1dff\u20d0-\u20ff\ufe20-\ufe2f]/gu, '')` at the very top of `normalizeInput`, BEFORE all other transformations. NFD decomposition first ensures precomposed chars (e.g. U+00E2 â) are broken into base char + combining mark (a + U+0302), then the strip removes the mark, leaving clean base char 'a'. Both call sites fixed (isOnTopic + hasInjectionInHistory both route through normalizeInput). All 7 test vectors pass: 4 bypass attempts now caught; 2 clean signals still detected; accented legitimate text (café→cafe) handled gracefully. (commit f8d2dee). Zero spawned agents found (sessions_list empty; three agents from ~21:40 MDT still never materialized). **Previous keepalive (2026-05-22 16:05 UTC, keepalive 140):** ⚡ **1 bug found and fixed.** `finalLat`/`finalLng` GPS strings were not normalized to pure numeric after the bounds check — `parseFloat` silently accepts non-numeric suffixes (e.g. `"35.123garbage"`, up to 20 chars via `.slice(0,20)`) during the bounds validation (line 1932) but the raw string was then stored as-is in sightings JSONL. While all current display paths use `parseFloat(s.lat)` so no XSS risk exists, storing garbage data could affect future code, and passing garbage to `reverseGeocode()` (via `encodeURIComponent`) sends invalid data to Nominatim API. Fixed: `finalLat = String(parseFloat(finalLat))` + `finalLng = String(parseFloat(finalLng))` added immediately after the bounds check passes — normalizes to clean numeric strings for all GPS sources (user form field, EXIF, proof.json) (commit f278ad3). **Previous keepalive (2026-05-22 02:45 UTC, keepalive 139):** ⚡ **1 bug found and fixed.** `proofEntry.getData()` in the Proofmode ZIP handler had no decompression size guard before `JSON.parse()`. The JPEG entry already had a 12MB zip-bomb guard (`jpegData.length > MAX_PHOTO_BYTES`), but the proof.json entry did not — a malicious ZIP (<12MB compressed) with a crafted proof.json could expand to hundreds of MB in RAM before the check, since ZIP compression ratios for repetitive JSON content can be 50:1 or more. Fixed: `proofEntry.header.size > MAX_PROOF_BYTES` (64KB) checked before `getData()` — throws 'proof.json exceeds size limit' caught by the outer ZIP error handler; real Proofmode proof.json is <2KB so this never affects legitimate submissions (commit 0a94dab). **Previous keepalive (2026-05-22 01:25 UTC, keepalive 137):** ⚡ **2 bugs found and fixed.** (1) ZIP decompression bomb in Proofmode bundle handler — `zip.readFile(jpegEntry)` read the full decompressed JPEG into RAM with no size cap; the 12MB limit applied only to the compressed `.zip` on upload, so a maliciously crafted ZIP bomb (<12MB compressed but GB+ decompressed) would exhaust RAM and disk before C2PA/EXIF checks ran. Fixed: `if (jpegData.length > MAX_PHOTO_BYTES) throw new Error('decompressed JPEG exceeds size limit')` after `readFile()` (commit b466df6). (2) busboy multipart handler missing `fields` and `fieldSize` limits — busboy defaults allow 1000 fields × 64KB each = ~64MB in the `fields` object per request; even rate-limited (10/min), this is a memory pressure vector. Fixed: `fields: 20` (sighting form uses ~7) + `fieldSize: 4096` (generous for all coord/note/type values) (commit b466df6). Zero spawned agents found (sessions_list empty). **Previous keepalive (2026-05-22 00:52 UTC, keepalive 136):** ⚡ **3 bugs found and fixed.** (1) `parseBody()` missing `req.destroy()` on 20KB size exceeded — after `reject()` was called, `data` events kept firing and `body += chunk` continued accumulating memory until the stream ended; a client sending a 100MB body would be fully buffered in RAM despite the 20KB rejection. Fixed: `req.destroy()` added before `reject()` (consistent with chat endpoint which already did this); subsequent error event from destroy() tries to call `reject()` again but is a no-op since Promise is already settled (commit 82f95e9). (2) No `server.requestTimeout` or `server.headersTimeout` — Caddy Caddyfile has no `reverse_proxy` timeout either; a client sending headers but never completing the request body (Slowloris-style) would hang `parseBody` and multipart handlers indefinitely. Fixed: `server.requestTimeout = 30000` (auto-responds 408 after 30s) + `server.headersTimeout = 15000` (auto-responds 408 if headers stall); both supported on Node 20.20.2 (commit 82f95e9). (3) `_proofLat`/`_proofLng` GPS injection via multipart form fields — busboy `field` handler accepted all user-submitted form fields including `_proofLat` and `_proofLng` (server-only keys set exclusively during ZIP proof.json extraction); a user with a valid C2PA-verified JPEG (no GPS EXIF) could submit `_proofLat=40.7128` + `_proofLng=-74.0060` as form fields to place their camera sighting at any arbitrary GPS location worldwide, bypassing `isNewCamera` proximity check. Fixed: `_proofLat`/`_proofLng` filtered from busboy field handler — only trusted when set by server ZIP extraction (commit 04b3ad3). Zero spawned agents found (sessions_list empty). **Previous keepalive (2026-05-21 22:19 UTC, keepalive 135):** ⚡ **1 bug found and fixed.** `processNext()` chat queue had 3 related issues: (1) No `ollama.on('error')` handler — if the Ollama response stream emitted an error mid-response (network blip, Ollama restart), `processing` stayed `true` forever, deadlocking the queue and silently rejecting all future AI chat requests; (2) No `res.on('close')` guard — if the browser client disconnected mid-stream, Ollama kept processing and streaming to nobody, wasting CPU/memory until it finished (could delay next queued request by the full Ollama inference time); (3) No idempotency guard — if both `ollama 'end'` and `ollama 'error'` fired for the same request (e.g., stream ends then socket errors), `processNext()` would be called twice, potentially starting two Ollama requests simultaneously. Fixed: added `settle()` closure with boolean `settled` flag ensuring processing resets exactly once per queued item; `ollama.on('error', settle)` handles stream errors cleanly; `res.on('close', () => { ollama.destroy(); settle() })` short-circuits wasted compute on disconnect; `res.headersSent` guard on `proxy.on('error')` prevents double-writeHead if headers already sent (commit f0fae2a). **Previous keepalive (2026-05-19 15:23 UTC, keepalive 128):** ⚡ **1 bug found and fixed.** `reset-password` handler used non-atomic `SELECT * FROM recovery_tokens WHERE id = ?` then `UPDATE SET used=1 WHERE id=?` — the async `bcrypt.compare()` call between SELECT and UPDATE created a TOCTOU race window where two concurrent requests with the same token could both pass the `row.used` check, both complete bcrypt, and both reset the password. Fixed: SELECT now uses `AND used=0`, atomic burn `UPDATE SET used=1 WHERE id=? AND used=0` runs BEFORE bcrypt (same pattern as claim_tokens), `.changes===0` guard handles race losers (commit cabe273). **Previous keepalive (2026-05-19 12:23 UTC, keepalive 126):** ⚡ **2 bugs found and fixed.** (1) `forgot-username` catch block missing `!res.headersSent` guard — when `parseBody` threw 'bad json' (empty/no body, e.g. `Content-Length: 0`), `res.end()` was never called and the connection hung indefinitely (confirmed via VPS logs: two 'forgot-username error: bad json' entries at 08:44+08:51 UTC from test requests). Added `if (!res.headersSent)` guard sending 200+ok message, maintaining always-OK security property. (2) `account/recover` catch block returned 500 ('Server error') when `parseBody` threw — inconsistent with stated 'Always respond OK' security goal. Fixed to return 200 with the standard recovery message when `!res.headersSent`. Both fixes commit 53935e5+4153243. **Previous keepalive (2026-05-18 23:47 UTC, keepalive 122):** ⚡ **2 bugs found and fixed.** (1) `parseCookies()` used `decodeURIComponent` without try/catch — a malformed cookie header (e.g. `%ZZ`) would throw `URIError`; `verifyToken` wrapped it safely but `verifyAdminSession` + `revokeAdminSession` did not, making any admin route susceptible to a request-crash DoS via crafted cookie. Fixed: fallback to raw value on URIError. (2) `reauthSessions` Map was missing from the 10-min GC interval — expired entries (userId → reauthUntil timestamp) accumulated indefinitely; low severity given 3 users but a correctness issue. Fixed: added to GC sweep. ## What Broke This Morning (2026-05-10) + What Was Fixed

### Root Cause
The overnight session (05-09 21:35-05-10 04:30) migrated ALL 1,585 inline styles to CSS classes in `App.css`. But `App.css` was **never imported** into the build. Result: 9,134 lines of component CSS were silently ignored - site rendered as naked HTML.

### Fixes Shipped (commits in order)
1. `6df7600` - `import './App.css'` added to App.jsx (was never there)
2. `42874d3` - Default theme COLD (dark), localStorage persistence restored (was hardcoded PRESS light with no persistence)
3. `f5e28b9` - `.nav-desktop { display:flex }` restored - primary nav links were invisible
4. `fcc5859` - Red hero tagline banner removed; Fund a Campaign → red; scrollbars → dark
5. `60cac6b` - Log In + Join → identical ghost button style

### Comprehensive CSS Audit Result
Autonomous audit of all 43 components confirmed: nav, hero, campaigns, cards, modals, admin, sighting form - all structurally intact. Only 2 minor gaps found (campaign filter buttons + HumanRegistry role buttons) - both already correct in App.css.

### Still Possibly Off (Scott hasn't done full QA yet)
- Cosmetic details Scott will find on scroll-through
- Fix in batches from screenshots - don't do one-at-a-time

## What's Solid (Don't Re-Audit)
- **Security:** Rate limits on all endpoints (incl. logout + logout-all added 2026-05-10 keepalive 7), CSP hardened (unsafe-inline removed), passkeys, bcrypt, JWT, timing-safe login, AES-256-GCM encrypted recovery emails, admin IP-bound sessions, fail2ban on VPS, SSH password auth disabled
- **SSRF:** AI proxy hardcoded to 127.0.0.1:11435; CA Bar lookup locked to apps.calbar.ca.gov only; body size 20KB JSON / 12MB photo
- **ZIP uploads:** AdmZip.readFile() (not extractEntryTo) - path traversal protected
- **AI proxy:** Queue max 5, injection scan across ALL messages (multi-turn bypass prevention), 4000 char message cap
- **CSS Migration:** 0 inline styles remaining - all in App.css (now imported)
- **Accessibility:** All form inputs have labels/aria-labels (CampaignList sort, CameraMap state, AdminPanel inputs - fixed 2026-05-10)
- **Server features:** All campaigns/proposals/registry admin endpoints, single-campaign API, forgot-username, health endpoint, tier-up + milestone emails, reverse geocode on sightings
- **VPS hardening:** Auto security updates, sysctl, daily backups, WAL checkpoint, graceful shutdown
- **Audit score: ~9.7/10** (reports in `docs/internal/`)

## Site Architecture
- React + Vite SPA → Netlify (static)
- Node.js/Express server.js → Hetzner VPS (AI proxy only - NOT deployed to Netlify)
- SQLite DB on VPS
- GitHub: `citeback/citebackwebsite` → auto-deploys to `heroic-yeot-51eaeb` (citeback@proton.me Netlify account)
- AI: Ollama qwen2.5:7b on VPS, proxied through Node at localhost:11435, Caddy → ai.citeback.com
